### Direct Join Names (ManyToOne/OneToOne)

Use these field names directly as join names in QL queries.

## Usage in QL Queries

### Entity Reference

```typescript
// Use the QL full name format: module.EntityName
start: {
  type: 'entity',
  name: 'bm.Invoice',  // From QL Name column
  as: 'e'
}
```

### Direct Join (ManyToOne/OneToOne)

```typescript
// Use the relationship field name as the join name
joins: [
  {
    type: 'entity',
    name: 'customer',  // Direct relationship field name
    as: 'c',
    joinType: 'left'
  }
]
```

### Reverse Join (OneToMany)

```typescript
// Use module.Entity#attributeName format for reverse relationships
// Based on MetaService.deriveJoins(): type.getAlias() + "#" + attribute.getName()
// Example: CustomerBillingAccount has reverse rel to CustomerBillingAccountBalance
joins: [
  {
    type: 'entity',
    name: 'bm.CustomerBillingAccountBalance#customerBillingAccount',  // Entities pointing TO this one
    as: 'bal',
    joinType: 'left',
    onlyFirst: true  // Often used with reverse joins to get single record
  }
]
```
